| Hard Line                                 | Hard-driven line attack; distinct from High Line's deep finesse shot                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| Jumbo Cross Court                         | Extreme cross-court angle (wider than hard angle)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| Joust                                     | Opposing players contacting the ball simultaneously at the net                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| Free Ball                                 | Easy over-the-net ball the receiving team can pass cleanly                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| Down Ball                                 | Standing spike from the attacker (no jump)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| Pepper                                    | Cooperative back-and-forth drill: dig / set / attack cycle                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| Speed Pepper                              | Pepper at higher tempo, pushing dig + set + attack speed                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| Speed Ball                                | Rapid sequential feed/serve format designed to keep the receiver moving continuously from ball to ball                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| Off Foot                                  | In setting footwork, the foot away from the net                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| Net Foot                                  | In setting footwork, the foot closest to the net                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| Off Pass                                  | Pass that pulls the setter away from the ideal setting window, often 15–20 ft off the net in BAB Plan 6                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| Back Set                                  | Set delivered behind the setter to the target / hitter                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| Run-through Set                           | Correction set made while running through the ball rather than stopping in ideal setting posture                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| Correction Set                            | Set made from a non-ideal pass location, including off-net or off-court passes                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| Defensive Retreatment                     | Dig-set-retreat pattern where the player sets back to the attacker, retreats from net, stops, and digs again                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| Wash Drill                                | Multi-ball scoring cycle where a team must convert a sequence of balls before switching                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| Open Net                                  | Attack phase with no defense; in Plan 6, the attack scores as long as it is in and does not hit the net                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| Mini Games                                | Modified game-play format with a score target and a specific first-ball or shot constraint                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| +3 / -3                                   | Score format: attack side needs +3 lead; defense needs -3. Used as a cross-skill scoring wrapper across BAB plans (pass quality in Plan 2; attack accuracy in Plan 7)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| 14–15 Games to 21                         | Score starts at 14–15 (choose who's up); play to 21                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| 3 Before 5                                | Pressure format: serving team scores 3 before receiving team scores 5                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| Quadrant                                  | A marked court zone used for footwork / contact constraints or serve-target sequencing                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| Seam                                      | The target channel between passers in pair serve-receive; in one-passer variants, this needs an explicit body-line or middle-zone definition                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| Sideline serve                            | Serve aimed near a passer's sideline shoulder / lane; tactically distinct from seam serving                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| Paradise                                  | The cross-court defense position you want to be in as a defender, watching the diagonal hitter. Canonical source: BAB Plan 12 Drill 3 (`4 Steps to Paradise`), which trains the footwork to transition between Paradise positions when the attack rotates sides                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| Open Net Swing                            | Attack swing taken with no blocker present on the other side; used in BAB Plan 7 Drill 5 to isolate hitting decision from blocker pressure                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| 4×4 box                                   | A square attack-accuracy target drawn at the high-line or cut-shot location; first introduced in BAB Plan 7 Drill 4 as the +3/-3 scoring target                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| Attack-accuracy box                       | More general term for a marked court rectangle used as an attack-target scoring zone (e.g., the high-line and cut-shot boxes in BAB Plan 7 Drills 4 and 6); distinct from BAB's 7-zone Around-the-World attack ladder and from FIVB's 5-zone attack convention                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| Short attack                              | An attack that intentionally lands close to the net (in BAB Plan 7 Drill 7, in front of a line drawn 15 ft from the net); used as a rule-delta on a normal point in competitive transition drills                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| Scrambled free ball                       | A free ball intentionally fed to a non-default location/player to force movement and quick reset; used in BAB Plan 7 Drill 6 to chain a high-line attack into an immediate cut-shot attempt by the partner                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| Comp Transition                           | BAB shorthand for "competitive transition" — pair-vs-pair sideout with a constraint rule on the first contact (BAB Plan 7 Drill 7)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| Bowls                                     | Coach-fed underhand initiating toss to start a sideout chain; treated as `partner-toss` for catalog purposes                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| Hitting a High Line / Cut Shot            | BAB technique-level per-shot drills (Plan 8 Drills 2 and 3): pass-set-attack the named shot while the tosser shifts to cross-court defense to read the shot; the simplest source form for per-shot attack technique                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| SHOTS ONLY                                | Rule restriction on a sideout-pressure drill: every attack must be a shot (no hard hits); used in BAB Plan 8 Drill 7 as a variant of `3 Before 5`                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| (only shots)                              | Lowercase variant of `SHOTS ONLY`; same restriction, used in BAB Plan 8 Drill 6 as a variant of `Comp Transition HL - CS - Live`                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| Round 1 and 2 ONLY                        | Rule restriction on a modified game: play only the first two rounds (Cut Shot, then High Line); used in BAB Plan 8 Drill 8 as a subset of `Mini Games to 7`                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| Per-shot variant                          | Authoring pattern observed across BAB attack drills (Plan 7 Drill 4, Plan 8 Drills 2/3, Plan 8 Drill 8 rounds, Plan 9 Drills 4/5): one drill record per named shot (HL, CS, Hard Angle, Hard Line, etc.) rather than one configurable parameterized drill                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| Rule-restricted variant                   | Authoring pattern observed across BAB Plan 8 (Drills 6, 7, 8): an existing drill family with a constraint overlay (`SHOTS ONLY`, `(only shots)`, `Round N ONLY`) that subsets the parent drill's behavior to keep practice on the named focus                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| Drill-name aliasing                       | Source observation from BAB Plan 9 (Drills 4 and 5): the same drill source form can carry different names across plans (Plan 8 `Hitting a High Line / Cut Shot` ≡ Plan 9 `Offensive Accuracy - HL / CS`); the cross-reference table maps multiple BAB names to a single future Volleycraft drill family                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| Vision pepper / look-and-react            | Pattern observed in BAB Plan 9 Drill 3 `3 Touch Vision Pepper`: the attacker must read the defender's hand position (up vs down) and choose where to drive; the defender's choice is communicated by hand placement, not call. Converges with FIVB's "quick look" cue (Drills 3.15 `Pass and Look`, 4.9 `Set and Look`)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| Beat the Blocker                          | BAB Plan 9 Drill 6 (name-only capture in this archive): an attack drill scored on placing the attack past a blocker on either the cross-court or line shot. Likely future provenance for a `blockerPresence: 'blocked'` attack drill, complementing Plan 7 Drill 5's open-net swing                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| 14-15 Games to 21                         | Compressed competitive game format: serving team starts at 15; play best-of-3/5/7. Tests practice work without a focus or shot constraint. Distinct from `Mini Games to 7` because it has no first-ball shot rule                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| Set to 21                                 | Full competitive set with side switches at 7s; the most game-realistic of the BAB-captured competitive wrappers. Tests whatever the practice has been working on                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| Competitive game wrapper                  | General term for BAB drills that score a normal or compressed game without a per-rep technique target (`14-15 Games to 21`, `Set to 21`); these are session-shape wrappers, not drills, and should not occupy the authoring-budget cap as drill records                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| Triangle Setting (4p hit-fed)             | BAB Plan 10 Drill 2: fourth Triangle Setting source form; 4-player hit-fed (P1 hits at P2, P3 and P4 alternate setting back); distinct from the 3-player versions in Plans 5/6/7 and from the 4-player serve-fed version in Plan 6 Drill 4. Carries an explicit level-scaled rule (Beginners catch / Intermediate-Advanced continuous)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| Serve to Free Ball                        | BAB Plan 10 Drill 3: pair-vs-pair drill that chains a serve-receive sideout and a free-ball-transition sideout to the **other** player; first BAB source for sideout-to-free-ball transition as a deliberate drill                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| Defender-role-differentiated drill family | Pattern observed in BAB Plan 10 Drills 4–7: same drill skeleton (serve to receiver, receiver hits a named shot, defense reacts) varies by attacker shot, blocker position, and defender pickup zone. The four drills together form a 3-axis matrix (shot × blocker-position × defender-pickup) with a **blocker-defender coupling rule** (when blocker takes line, defender takes cut shot; when blocker takes cross, defender takes highline)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| Blocker-defender coupling                 | BAB Plan 10 Drills 5–6 source: defender position is **relative to the blocker**, not absolute. The blocker-defender pair forms a single defensive unit. Beach-defense analog of the moving-triangle passing theory                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| Level-scaled rule                         | BAB Plan 10 Drill 2 source: a single drill description specifies different behaviors per level (Beginners catch after the set; Intermediate/Advanced make the drill continuous by hitting the set back to the passer). Distinct from per-level **parameter** scaling (e.g., Plan 2's 4/6/8 serving zones) — this is per-level **rule** scaling                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| Best of N                                 | BAB game-wrapper modifier (Plans 9, 10, 11): play a series of compressed games, best of 3 / 5 / 7. Plan 10 Drill 9 locks "Best of 3"; Plan 11 Drill 6 locks "Best of 5"; Plan 9 Drill 7's source text frames it as "best of 3/5/7"                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| Rule-augmented variant                    | Authoring pattern observed in BAB Plan 11 Drill 4: an existing drill family with an **additive** scoring rule (the blocker-touch -1 penalty added to Plan 7 Drill 4's `+3/-3 HL/CS`). Sibling but inverse to **rule-restricted variant** (Plan 8 patterns subset/restrict; Plan 11 Drill 4 augments/extends). Both fall under Thesis T9                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| Beat the Blocker (full source)            | BAB Plan 11 Drill 5 (full source detail): 4-player hard-hit attack drill where the blocker chooses among grab / block line / block cross and the attacker reads to challenge or avoid; two big squares on Line and Angle as scoring targets; "okay to get blocked" framing. Closes the Plan 9 Drill 6 name-only entry                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| Reactive blocker                          | BAB Plan 11 Drill 5 source: a blocker who **chooses** their action in real time (grab the ball, block line, or block cross) so the attacker must read and react. Distinct from the **fixed blocker** in Plan 10 Drills 5/6 where the blocker's position is named in the drill spec. Future Volleycraft attack metadata likely needs `blockerBehavior: 'fixed'                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| Line and Angle squares                    | BAB Plan 11 Drill 5 source: two large scoring rectangles drawn on the **line** and the **angle** — the two primary hard-hit targets. Distinct from the 4×4 attack-accuracy box (Plan 7 Drill 4) and from the two-shot HL+CS box geometry (Plan 7 Drill 6) because these score hard hits past a blocker, not finesse shots                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| Hard-driven shot / hard hit               | BAB language for a hard-hit attack (vs a finesse shot). Plan 11 Drill 5 explicitly says "hard-driven shot." Volleycraft authoring should treat hard hits and shots as separate attack subkinds for workload accounting (`D77`) and success-metric design                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| Crossover step                            | One step in BAB defensive footwork: the foot away from the dig direction crosses over the other foot to start lateral movement. Used in BAB Plan 12 Drill 2 (`Partner Toss Dig to Cut Shot`, "one crossover step plus laydown/dive") and Drill 3 (`4 Steps to Paradise`, the first of the four steps)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| Laydown / dive                            | BAB defensive emergency dig technique: the defender extends low to the ground (laydown) or commits a full dive to reach a ball just out of normal reach. Used in BAB Plan 12 Drill 2 paired with the crossover step                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| Antenna height                            | BAB target trajectory for a defensive dig: lift the dig high enough to reach antenna height so the setter can comfortably play the next ball. Source: BAB Plan 12 Drill 2 ("at contact you are lifting your dig to antenna height")                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| 4 Steps                                   | BAB defensive movement sequence: crossover → step → plant → plant. The prescribed footwork to transition between cross-court defense positions when the attack rotates sides. Source: BAB Plan 12 Drill 3 (`4 Steps to Paradise`). Defense-side analog of setting's off-foot/net-foot footwork (Plan 5 Drill 2)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| Cross-court defense position              | The diagonal position a defender takes when the opposing attacker is on the opposite side; the defender watches the diagonal hitter from this position. BAB calls it "Paradise"; Plan 12 Drill 3 trains the movement between these positions                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| Drill-repurposing across focus            | BAB authoring pattern observed in Plans 12 and 13: a single drill (e.g., `Serve a Spot - Dig Set Hit`, `Mini Games to 7`, `Hitting a HL/CS` ≡ `Toss to HL/CS`) appears in multiple practice plans with **different focus framing** rather than authoring a separate drill per focus area. The drill is unchanged; the practice context frames the emphasis (Plan 13 makes this most explicit by re-naming the per-shot HL/CS drills from attacker-perspective to defender-perspective). Converges with Thesis T1 in `docs/research/practice-plan-authoring-synthesis.md` (focus is purpose, not a tag)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| Defense plan grammar                      | BAB defensive plan structure observed in Plans 12-13: warm-up → per-shot dig technique → defensive movement → integrated chain → competitive game wrapper. Mirrors the attack plan grammar (Plans 7-11) and the setting plan grammar (Plans 5-6) at the structural level — confirming the BAB practice-plan template is focus-agnostic at the structural level                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| Dig from Knees                            | BAB Plan 13 Drill 2: isolated emergency-extension defensive drill where the defender starts on knees, lays down, and one-handed-scoop-digs a low ball (below net height) tossed by a partner. Trains the lowest-reach scoop motion at calibrated trajectory                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| Sand angel                                | BAB Plan 13 Drill 2 pre-drill ritual: the player lays flat in the sand and stretches arms and legs out to mark their physical reach radius from a knees-down starting position. Calibrates the player to where they can and cannot reach a ball before the drill starts                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| One-handed scoop dig                      | BAB Plan 13 Drill 2 technique: a low-ball emergency dig where the defender extends one hand under the ball with a scooping motion to lift it back over the net. Distinct from platform dig (forearms together) and hand dig (overhand). Used when the ball is below net height and out of platform reach                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| Hand dig                                  | BAB Plan 13 Drill 4 technique: an overhand defensive contact against a hard-hit ball at chest or head height. Uses hands rather than platform/forearms. Distinct from FIVB's `tomahawk` (passing-emergency two-hand overhead touch on a serve at face); same physical motion, different scenario                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| Platform dig                              | The standard forearm dig, contrasted in BAB Plan 13 Drill 4 with hand dig. Distinct technique selection: platform for low/medium balls, hand dig for high/hard balls at chest/head. Already implicit across earlier BAB drills; Plan 13 makes the platform-vs-hand distinction explicit                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| Release back to defense                   | BAB Plan 13 Drill 4 transition motion: after a defender contributes a contact (dig or set), they immediately move back to defensive position to receive the next attack. Trains continuous defensive engagement rather than isolated single-rep technique                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| Defender-perspective framing              | BAB authoring pattern observed in Plan 13 Drills 5–6: the same drill source form as Plans 8/9 per-shot HL/CS technique drills, but the explanation re-frames the named focus character from attacker (`Player 2 hits a high-line shot`) to defender (`Player 1 reacts and catches shot`). Drill is unchanged; practice context shifts from attack-focus to defense-focus. Strongest BAB evidence yet for Thesis T1 drill-repurposing across focus                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| Pull into line / Pull into angle          | BAB Plan 14 Drill 3 named scenarios: the blocker disengages from the net into either the line lane (line) or the angle lane (angle) to play defense. The two scenarios train different defensive coverage zones from the same starting position. Source spelling note: Plan 14 has typo "angel" — canonical archive spelling is "angle"                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| Transition setting                        | BAB Plan 14 named pattern: a player who just contributed a previous defensive contact (dig or block) becomes the setter on the third contact. Distinct from dedicated-setter drills because the setter role is dynamic within the rally.
