Plan 14 Drills 3 (set-back-to-blocker variant), 4, and 5 all use this pattern explicitly                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| Smack                                     | BAB Plan 14 Drills 4–5 attacker action: a deliberate vocal/visual cue that fakes a hard hit, telling the defender "hit incoming." Followed in the same source by a toss for a retrievable shot — the smack is misdirection, not a real attack                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| Smack-then-toss / Smack misdirection      | BAB Plan 14 Drills 4–5 deceptive feed pattern: the attacker smacks the ball (fake hard hit) then actually tosses a finesse shot. Trains defenders to read late and change direction. Distinct feed pattern from `partner-toss` (no fake), `live-serve` (real serve), or `scrambled free ball` (no fake, just non-default placement). Future Volleycraft drill metadata may need a `feedPattern` field separate from `feedType`                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| Change direction late                     | BAB Plan 14 Drills 4–5 defensive technique: detecting that a smack was a fake before final contact, aborting the wrong-direction shuffle, and pivoting to dig the actual shot. Trains defensive late-read against attacker deception                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| Attacker-deception read drill             | Pattern observed in BAB Plan 14 Drills 4–5: a read drill where the **attacker** is the deceiver (via smack-misdirection) rather than the defender (Plan 9 Drill 3 `3 Touch Vision Pepper`) or the blocker (Plan 11 Drill 5 `Beat the Blocker`). The deceiver-role rotation across these three plans suggests `deceiverRole: 'defender'                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| Win by 2                                  | BAB Plan 15 Drill 7 scoring extension: a standard volleyball game-extension rule where the winning team must reach the target score with at least a 2-point lead. First BAB capture that names this rule explicitly. Future Volleycraft scoring metadata should support composable scoring rules (base scoring format + extension)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| Live-point integration                    | Recurring BAB plan-grammar pattern observed in multiple plans: a controlled-feed technique drill is paired with a live-point integration drill that takes the same target shot or scenario into a live point. Captured pairs: per-shot HL/CS (Plans 8/9) → Comp Transition Live (Plan 7 Drill 7); Shuffle to HL/CS Dig (Plan 14) → Shuffle to HL/CS to Live Play (Plan 15 Drill 6). Future Volleycraft session-builder logic could expose this as a sequencing rule that groups paired drills in adjacent slots when both are catalog-active                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| Vision (defender read concept)            | BAB cross-drill cue meaning "read the defender / opposing court before contact." Used as a drill family marker in Plan 9 Drill 3 (`3 Touch Vision Pepper`) and as a coaching cue in Plan 15 Drill 7 ("use vision to score"). Future Volleycraft drill copy should treat "vision" as a defender-read concept that applies across multiple drill subkinds, not just one drill                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| Threat or No Threat                       | BAB Plan 16 Drills 5–6 read drill: the blocker reads **set quality** (a teammate's contact) and decides between two committed defensive actions — block (good set = THREAT) or pull off net to dig (bad set = NOT a threat). First BAB source for a **blocker-as-reader** drill where the read cue is team-context (set quality) rather than opponent action                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| Blocker-as-reader                         | Read-drill subkind where the BLOCKER is the read-and-decide actor (not the deceiver, not a passive blocker). Distinct from earlier read drills where the attacker reads (Plans 9, 11) or the defender reads (Plan 14). First BAB source: Plan 16 Drills 5–6. Adds a new `readerRole` axis to the read-drill schema, distinct from the `deceiverRole` axis from Thesis T11                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| Block vs Pull                             | BAB Plan 16 Drills 5–6 binary decision: the blocker either commits to blocking at the net or pulls off the net to dig. The decision is driven by set quality (THREAT vs NOT-A-THREAT). Combines Plan 14's `Pull Digs to Set` technique foundation with a decision-making overlay                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| Set quality (read cue)                    | BAB Plan 16 Drills 5–6 cue source: the **quality of a teammate's set** (good vs bad / off the net) is the cue the blocker reads to decide block vs pull. First BAB capture where the read cue is a **team-context cue** (teammate's contact quality) rather than an opponent action. Future Volleycraft attack/defense content should distinguish opponent-action cues from team-context cues in read-drill metadata                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| Toss-fed → serve-fed sibling pair         | BAB authoring pattern observed in Plan 3 Drills 4–5 (`Passing Triangle from Toss/Serve`) and Plan 16 Drills 5–6 (`Threat or No Threat` toss-fed and serve-fed): the same drill structure paired across two feed types, with no other structural difference. Distinct from the controlled-feed → live-point integration pattern (where the second variant adds live-point play, not just a feed change). Future Volleycraft drill metadata should support this pairing as variants on a single parent drill                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| Best of 3, Match to 21                    | BAB Plan 16 Drill 7 competitive wrapper format: full volleyball match playing to 21, best-of-3 series, with a `third-to-15` tiebreaker rule. Distinct from `14-15 Games to 21` (compressed scoring), `Set to 21` (single set), and the `Mini Games to 7` family (multi-round modified games)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| Third-to-15 tiebreaker                    | BAB Plan 16 Drill 7 scoring rule: in a best-of-3 series, if the match goes to a deciding third game, that third game is played to 15 instead of 21. Composable with Plan 15's `win by 2` extension. Together with `win by 2`, they confirm that game-wrapper scoring should be modeled as composable parameters: base game-to-N + tiebreaker-to-M + win-by-margin extension as three independent rules                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| Composable scoring rules                  | Source-evidenced authoring pattern from Plans 15 (`win by 2`), 16 (`third-to-15`), and 17 (`BIG point`, `switch sides after 2 BIG points`, `final set to 15 regardless`): game-wrapper scoring is built from independent rule fragments. Plan 17 expands the captured set to **at least six composable rule kinds**: (1) base score-to-N, (2) tiebreaker-to-M, (3) win-by-margin extension, (4) side-switch trigger, (5) outcome-elevation gate, and (6) conditional-extension-if-time-allows. Future Volleycraft scoring metadata should support these as six independent parameters rather than enumerating each combination as a separate scoring type                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| Race to 5 (HL and CS)                     | BAB Plan 17 Drill 3 competitive race format: **two role-symmetric attackers** (both left sides) race to 5 in-the-box accuracy shots, alternating via a single server's feed and a single setter. Round 1 high line; Round 2 cut shot. First BAB drill with **two competing attackers in role-symmetric structure** (distinct from Plan 5 Drill 8's two-attacker battle and from Plan 8's per-shot single-attacker pairs). Sibling per-shot variants per Thesis T8                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| 10 Sideouts                               | BAB Plan 17 Drill 4 measurement format: each player gets 10 serves in a row to side out **against a full defense** (blocker + defender on serving side); track each player's score for competitive comparison. **First BAB drill explicitly using "successful reps in a fixed trial count" measurement mode** (FIVB Level I Coaches Manual Ch VII p. 122). The trial cap is per-player (10 serves), and the metric is naturally a sideout-rate. Strongest cross-source convergence to date with FIVB measurement-mode taxonomy                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| BIG point                                 | BAB Plan 17 Drill 5 outcome-elevation rule: in the `3 Before 5` base drill, achieving the win condition (5 sideouts before 3 stops) **does not directly score**; instead, it earns the right to a serve-and-win sub-game whose result is what scores. Winning the sub-game = 1 BIG point; play to 3-4 BIG points. **Fourth composable scoring-overlay rule kind** alongside rule-restriction (Plan 8), rule-augmentation (Plans 11/15), and tiebreaker (Plan 16). Distinct because it gates the win condition behind a sub-game rather than narrowing or augmenting the parent drill's behavior                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| Side-switch trigger                       | BAB scoring rule across multiple plans: switch court sides at a specific score-event trigger to balance environmental factors (sun, wind). Plan 9 Drill 8 `Set to 21` uses "switch at 7s"; Plan 17 Drill 5 uses "switch sides after 2 BIG points." Independent composable rule fragment (axis 4 of the captured 6-kind scoring grammar)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| Outcome elevation (scoring rule)          | Composable scoring-rule kind first captured in BAB Plan 17 Drill 5: achieving the parent drill's win condition triggers a sub-game whose outcome is what actually scores. Distinct from rule-restriction (subsets behavior), rule-augmentation (extends behavior), and tiebreaker (extends only when match is tied). Future Volleycraft scoring metadata should treat this as the fourth composable rule kind                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| Conditional extension                     | BAB scoring rule first explicit in Plan 17 Drill 6 `Games to 21`: "if you have time, complete the final set to 15 regardless of who wins or losses." Distinct from tiebreaker (which extends only when match is tied) and from win-by-margin (which extends only when the target is reached without margin). The extension is **conditioned on time-remaining**, not on match state. Future Volleycraft session-builder logic could distinguish "scheduled" vs "if-time-allows" wrapper extensions                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| Match to 21                               | BAB Plan 17 Drill 6 wrapper format: traditional beach volleyball match scoring. Distinct from compressed wrappers (`14-15 Games to 21`), single-set wrappers (`Set to 21`), best-of-N wrappers (`Best of 3, Match to 21`), and modified games (`Mini Games to 7`). Plan 17 frames it with a conditional-extension rule (final set to 15 if time allows)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| Game Play cluster                         | BAB drill-book ordering: Plans 17–20 are the **Game Play cluster**, the fifth and final single-focus cluster after passing (1–4), setting (5–6), attacking (7–11), and defense (12–16). Plan 17 is the first Game Play plan captured at source-detail level. The 2026-05-04 founder capture labeled Plan 17 as "defensive," which is inconsistent with BAB's drill-book TOC and with Plan 17's drill content (race-to-N, sideout-rate measurement, BIG point gate, full-match wrapper); future captures from Plans 18–20 should resolve any remaining cluster-labeling ambiguity                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| Participant structure                     | Source-evidenced schema axis from Plan 17 Drill 3: drills with **role-symmetric competing participants** (two attackers racing to 5) are structurally distinct from drills with **role-differentiated participants** (server / passer / setter / target) or **role-symmetric cooperative participants** (cooperative pepper). Future Volleycraft drill metadata may need a `participantStructure` axis distinguishing these three structures, separately from `participants.min/max` which counts seats, not relations                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| Add In / Add Out                          | BAB Plan 18 Drill 5 wash-drill scoring rule: the **only** way to earn a point is by winning a consecutive serve-receive ball **AND** a serve ball; if a team wins one but not the other, the points "wash" and neither team scores. "Add In" describes the receive-half (sideout adds a point on receive); "Add Out" describes the serve-half (break point adds a point on serve). 4-serve rotation A1, B1, B2, A2 ensures both teams have equal serve and receive opportunities per cycle. **First BAB source detail for conjunctive / wash scoring** as a structural pattern (Plan 6 Drill 7's `Open Net, High Line, Free. Wash Drill` was the first BAB use of the term but did not specify the scoring mechanics)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| Wash drill (full source)                  | BAB drill format where points only score when both halves of a multi-event sequence are won by the same team; if the conditions split, the result "washes" and no points are scored. **First source-detail capture in Plan 18 Drill 5 (`Add In/Add Out`).** Distinct from rule-restriction (subsets behavior), rule-augmentation (extends behavior with a penalty/bonus), tiebreaker (extends only on tie), and outcome-elevation (sub-game gates the score) — wash scoring is **conjunctive with cancellation**. Adds a seventh composable scoring rule kind to the captured set                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| Conjunctive / wash scoring                | Composable scoring-rule kind first source-detail-captured in BAB Plan 18 Drill 5 (`Add In/Add Out`): a point scores only on the conjunction of two independent conditions; if one condition is met but not the other, the result is a wash (no points either way). Distinct from sequential dependency (Plan 17's outcome-elevation gate where a sub-game *follows* the parent drill's win condition) — wash conditions are **concurrent independent halves**. Future Volleycraft scoring metadata should treat conjunctive/wash scoring as a distinct rule kind alongside the six earlier-captured kinds (rule-restriction, rule-augmentation, tiebreaker, side-switch trigger, outcome-elevation gate, conditional-extension-if-time-allows)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| Triangle Setting (Serve)                  | BAB Plan 6 Drill 4 / Plan 18 Drill 3: 4-player serve-fed Triangle Setting variant. P1 serves; P2 passes; P3 sets; P4 is the target for the set. 8 serves per side, rotate. Distinct from the 4-player hit-fed Triangle Setting (Plans 10, 11, 14) because the feed is a serve, providing full serve-receive context. Two BAB plan references (Plans 6, 18). Sibling feed-type variant of `Triangle Setting (4p hit-fed)` per Thesis T8                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| Triangle Setting with Attack (Serve)      | BAB Plan 18 Drill 4: **first whole-chain Triangle Setting variant**. P1 serves; P2 **passes AND hits** the set; P3 and P4 set. Adds attack as the third contact, completing the sideout chain. Distinct from prior Triangle Setting variants (which all stopped at the set). The single-passer-attacker workload pattern is **beach-realistic** because the receiving team has only 2 players. New chain-completion sibling variant on the Triangle Setting family; first BAB source for participant-role-transition within Triangle Setting                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| Single-passer-attacker workload pattern   | Source-evidenced beach-realistic pattern across multiple BAB drills: the same player contributes two contacts in different roles within a sideout chain (pass → attack with same player). Captured cases: Plan 10 Drill 7 (hard cross from a serve, receiver hits), Plan 14 Drill 3 (Pull Digs to Set, transition-setting variant where the blocker becomes the setter), Plan 17 Drill 5 (3 Before 5 chained per-player), and Plan 18 Drill 4 (Triangle Setting with Attack — P2 passes AND hits). Future Volleycraft drill metadata may need a participant-role-transition axis to capture this pattern symmetrically across drills                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| Game Play cluster grammar                 | Recurring within-cluster structural pattern observed across BAB Plans 17, 18, and 19 (the three captured Game Play plans): opener (Best Warm Up Ever) → 4-player chain primer (Triangle Setting in Plans 17/18, Cross Court Pepper in Plan 19 — slot 2 is "any 4-player chain primer," not Triangle Setting only) → per-shot or per-skill technique under pressure → **slot 4 (movement) skipped** → decision/pressure overlay drill (10 Sideouts in Plan 17 / Triangle Setting with Attack in Plan 18 / Comp Transition HL/CS Live in Plan 19) → live-feed sideout drill with novel scoring rule (3 Before 5 with BIG points in Plan 17 / Add In/Add Out wash in Plan 18 / Small Court Mini Games to 7 with scoring-zone gate in Plan 19) → competitive wrapper (Games to 21 / 14-15 Games to 21 / Game to 21 base). Slot 4 (movement) intentionally skipped in all three Game Play plans — confirmed across three data points as a structural feature of the cluster grammar, not a Plan 17 anomaly. Plan 20 (uncaptured) is the final test for whether the slot-4-skip pattern holds across all four Game Play plans |
| Small Court: Mini Games to 7              | BAB Plan 19 Drill 5 modified-game format: line drawn down the center of the court dividing both sides into halves; designated scoring side decided before each game; **every point must be scored on the designated side, either left or right**, for the rally outcome to count. Drill also has a level-scaled rule (beginner/intermediate any-player serve; advanced same-player serve). Fifth documented Mini Games to 7 variant in the captured set, with **scoring-zone gate** as the new overlay rule kind                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| Scoring-zone gate                         | Composable scoring-rule kind first source-detail-captured in BAB Plan 19 Drill 5 (`Small Court: Mini Games to 7`): points only score when the rally terminates with a specific spatial outcome (e.g., the ball lands on the designated half of the court). Distinct from rule-restriction (which constrains *behavior* — players still hit anywhere; only the outcome zone matters), outcome-elevation (no sub-game), and conjunctive/wash (no multi-event conjunction). **Eighth composable scoring rule kind** in the captured BAB grammar. Future Volleycraft `successMetric` taxonomy needs an outcome-spatial-condition metric shape distinct from `reps-successful` (cumulative single events) and `points-to-target` (numeric threshold)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| Game to 21 (base form)                    | BAB Plan 19 Drill 6 wrapper format: "Normal set to 21 with no regulations." **Cleanest minimal-overlay base form** of the Games to 21 wrapper family. Confirms BAB has both base forms (this) and overlay variants (Plan 9 Drill 8 `Set to 21` with side-switches at 7s; Plan 16 Drill 7 `Best of 3, Match to 21` with `third-to-15` tiebreaker; Plan 17 Drill 6 `Games to 21` with conditional-extension; Plan 18 Drill 6 `14-15 Games to 21, Best of 5` compressed-start with best-of-5; Plan 19 Drill 6 with no overlays). Future Volleycraft session-builder logic should treat the base form as the default and the eight composable rule kinds as opt-in overlays                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| Within-Game-Play slot 2 primer            | Source observation across Plans 17/18/19/20: the slot-2 primer in Game Play plans can be either Triangle Setting (4p hit-fed, Plans 17/18/20) or Cross Court Pepper (Plan 19) — both are 4-player drills that warm up the integrated chain. Plan 20 confirms Triangle Setting (4p hit-fed) is the more common primer in the captured Game Play cluster (3 of 4 plans). Future Game Play archetypes should support multiple primer choices with Triangle Setting (4p hit-fed) as the default                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| 16-18 Run with It                         | BAB Plan 20 Drill 5 pressure-game format: pair-vs-pair drill where Team A is the receiving team for the entire round, starts with 16 points, and must reach 21 by scoring **consecutively**. If Team A misses a point, the score resets to 16. Team B accumulates points normally — each point Team B wins adds to their score. Play until one team reaches 21. **Win by 2** if needed. Each team is the receive team 6 times, 3 on each side. The drill name describes the consecutive-streak requirement: you have to "run" with a streak from 16 to 21 without missing                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| Reset-on-miss scoring                     | Composable scoring-rule kind first source-detail-captured in BAB Plan 20 Drill 5 (`16-18 Run with It`): points only count toward the score if accumulated **consecutively**; missing a point resets the score to a starting threshold. **Ninth composable scoring rule kind** in the captured BAB grammar. Distinct from existing `successMetric.type: streak` because: streak-counting tracks consecutive successes without a numeric base; reset-on-miss requires reaching a numeric target (21) starting from a numeric base (16) by *not missing* across the entire run. Future Volleycraft `successMetric` taxonomy needs a new metric shape that combines streak-counting with floor-reset semantics                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| Asymmetric scoring                        | Source-evidenced scoring axis first captured in BAB Plan 20 Drill 5: different teams have different scoring rules in the same drill. Team A subject to reset-on-miss / consecutive-streak-required scoring; Team B subject to accumulating-normal scoring. **First BAB source for per-team-rule mechanism** — distinct from any prior captured rule kind because earlier rules applied symmetrically to both teams. Future Volleycraft scoring metadata needs an asymmetric-scoring axis: `scoringRules: { teamA: ..., teamB: ... }` rather than a single drill-level rule                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| Streak-with-floor-reset                   | Hybrid metric shape first captured in BAB Plan 20 Drill 5 (`16-18 Run with It`): a numeric target (21) must be reached starting from a numeric base/floor (16) via consecutive successes; any single miss resets the score to the floor. Combines streak-counting (consecutive successes) with floor-reset semantics (reset to base on miss). FIVB's "Successful reps in a row" measurement mode is the closest cross-source analog but typically lacks the explicit floor-reset target. Future Volleycraft `successMetric` taxonomy should support this as a distinct metric shape                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| Game Play cluster (complete)              | BAB drill-book ordering: Plans 17–20 are the Game Play cluster, the fifth and final single-focus cluster. **All four Game Play plans now captured at source-detail level (2026-05-04)** — the captured BAB drill book is structurally complete. The cluster shares: opener (Best Warm Up Ever), 4-player chain primer (Triangle Setting in 3-of-4 plans, Cross Court Pepper in 1), per-skill technique under pressure at slot 3 (attacking accuracy in Plan 17/19, setting in Plan 18, serving in Plan 20), **slot 4 (movement) skipped across all four plans**, decision/pressure overlay at slot 5 (sideout pressure / measurement / wash / comp transition), live-feed novel scoring overlay at slot 6 (BIG point / wash / scoring-zone gate / reset-on-miss), and competitive wrapper at slot 7 (Game-to-21 family). **T10 (read drills) is absent from the entire Game Play cluster** — confirmed narrowing of T10 from a universal pattern to a Defense/Attack-only pattern                                                                                                                                       |
| Captured BAB drill book (complete)        | As of 2026-05-04, all 20 BAB Drill Book practice plans are captured at source-detail level. The captured set contains ~30 distinct source forms accounting for ~140 drill slots across the 20 plans, confirming Thesis T13's "small unique inventory + many plans → forced reuse" reading. Most-repeated source forms: Best Warm Up Ever (18 plans, cluster-universal opener), Triangle Setting (4p hit-fed) (8 plans), 14-15 Games to 21 (8 plans), Comp Transition HL/CS Live (6 plans), Cross Court Pepper (5 plans), `3 Before 5` family (5 plans across three clusters), Around the World (Serve) (4 plans). The captured BAB scoring grammar has nine composable rule kinds plus asymmetric scoring as a tenth axis. Future BAB-related Volleycraft work should treat the captured set as the authoritative reference                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |


### Around the World — 7 attacking zones vs scalable serving zones

BAB uses "Around the World" as a drill-format template applied to both attacking and serving. The zone counts differ and are load-bearing for Tier 1 Unit 3:

- **Attacking (7 zones)**: Short Poke Line, Mid Line Power, High Line, Deep Middle, Jumbo Cross Court, Hard Angle, Cut Shot.
- **Serving (4 / 6 / 8 zones)**: Plan 2 scales quadrants by level: 4 beginner, 6 intermediate, 8 advanced. The current `d33` implementation uses the 6-zone form (front-left / front-middle / front-right / back-left / back-middle / back-right).

Tier 1 Unit 3 authors `d33 Around the World Serving` with **6 zones** to match the M001 middle form of BAB's serving convention. A future attack chain (Tier 3+) authors its own Around-the-World with 7 zones; a future serving polish pass can decide whether to expose the 4-zone and 8-zone scales.

## Source 2 — Beach Volleyball Beginner's Guide to Success

### Scope

- **Type**: BAB course with 4 lessons, each with short tutorials and homework drills
- **Target user**: Beginner beach player (or existing-sport player new to beach)
- **Pedagogical shape**: Every lesson has a fixed structure: **Tutorials** (3 per lesson average, 2–4 min of explanation each) + **Homework** (1–3 drills per lesson, explicit drill names).

### Lesson structure (captured verbatim)

**Lesson 1 — Passing / Serve Receive**

- Tutorials:
  - The Perfect Platform
  - Passing/Serve Receive — Footwork
- Homework drills:
  - 6 Legged Monster
  - 4 Quadrant Ball Control
  - One Person Quadrant Pass Set Kill

**Lesson 2 — Setting**

- Tutorials:
  - Setting — How to Bump Set
  - Setting — How to Hand Set
  - Setting — Principles (*Set your Hitter, NOT a spot on the court*)
- Homework drills:
  - Tutorial Drill: Footwork for Setting
  - Corner to Corner Setting

**Lesson 3 — Attacking**

- Tutorials:
  - Attacking — Footwork, Timing, and Spacing
  - Attacking — Arm Swing
  - Attacking — Finding the Attacking Corridor
- Homework drills: *(none captured in the source paste — lesson has tutorials only or the homework section was not included)*

**Lesson 4 — Serving**

- Tutorials:
  - Serving — 3 Different Types of Serves
  - Serving — How to Standing Float Serve
  - Serving — What's Your Mission?
- Homework drills:
  - Self Toss Target Practice

### Invariants pulled from this source

Promoted into `coachingCues` and courtside copy in Tier 1 Units 3 and 4:

- **Setting principle #1**: *"Set your hitter, not a spot on the court."* Lives on all pair setting drills (`d42` Partner Set Back-and-Forth and up in the 8-drill Tier 1 Unit 4 chain).
- **Setting principle #2**: *"Triangle hands. High and stable."* From the Hand Set tutorial. Lives on Hand Set Fundamentals + Triangle Setting drills.
- **Serving principle #1**: *"What's your mission?"* From the Serving-Mission tutorial. Lives as an intent cue across all serving rungs 2–7.
- **Serving taxonomy**: *"Three types of serves: standing float, jump float, jump topspin."* Lives as a taxonomy header comment on `chain-6-serving` in `app/src/data/progressions.ts` so future authors don't mix topspin into the float ladder without an explicit rung.

### Drill-name anchors pulled from this source

- `Self Toss Target Practice` — canonical BAB name for the serving rung 1 drill (used as the name of `d31` in Tier 1 Unit 3).
- `Footwork for Setting` — canonical BAB name, already used as the name of the setting-chain footwork rung.
- `Corner to Corner Setting` — canonical BAB name, already used.
- `Bump Set` vs `Hand Set` — BAB treats these as two separately-taught fundamentals. Tier 1 Unit 4 splits the setting-chain foundation rung accordingly (see cross-reference below).

### Drill-name candidates (not in Tier 1)

Deferred to content polish / Tier 2+ authoring:

- `6 Legged Monster` — pair passing drill; already appears in Practice Plan 4 of the drill book.
- `4 Quadrant Ball Control` — solo-friendly ball control drill.
- `One Person Quadrant Pass Set Kill` — solo self-toss full-rep drill (pass → set → kill from one person). Novel relative to the drill book.

## Source 3 — Coaches Guide: How to Prepare the Perfect Beach Volleyball Practice

### Scope

Selected verbatim excerpts, the practice-plan template, and summaries captured from the BAB Coaches Guide:

1. Establishing a Focus
2. Engaging Your Team and Keeping Them Engaged (includes the canonical Practice Plan Template)
3. Keeping the Competitive Fire Throughout Practice

### Essay 1 — Establishing a Focus (summary + load-bearing quotes)

Core claim (load-bearing for the single-focus invariant in `app/src/data/archetypes.ts`):

> "It's crucial that all drills during the practice are designed to reinforce this focus. A common mistake is creating drills that don't align with the intended focus, leading to a scattered practice. By maintaining a consistent focus, your athletes will have a specific skill to work on throughout the session."

> "Having a clear vision also helps you manage any drop in performance during practice. If the level of play decreases, you can bring the group back to the focal point of the session."

Tier 1 use: cited in the `app/src/data/archetypes.ts` invariant 1 header comment and in the `Pass · Serve · Set` single-focus toggle's rationale (`docs/plans/2026-04-20-m001-tier1-implementation.md` Unit 4). **2026-05-04 promote-and-revert provenance.** This essay's *"all drills designed to reinforce this focus"* claim was provisionally promoted to a canonical decision (`D136`, single-focus-per-session invariant) on 2026-05-04 and reverted same-day after the `ce-product-lens-reviewer` review surfaced that BAB Plan 1 (captured verbatim in this document, Drills 1–8, especially Drills 4–7) actually argues for *integrative-goal* focus — a passing-focus session served by setting and attack drills under that focus — rather than the *skill-isolation* focus the provisional `D136` enforced via the selection path. The promotion conflated two claims that diverge on source inspection: (i) the descriptive claim that the in-code selection path enforces single-chain per slot, and (ii) the aspirational claim about session-level focus coherence. The single-focus-per-session intuition continues to live as a code-level invariant in `app/src/data/archetypes.ts` (invariant 1) and as a Tier 1 plan reference; whether to promote it (and in what shape — selection-path-narrow vs session-coherence-broad) is now tracked as `O24`. The level-refinement intuition (beginner focus broad, advanced focus narrow) continues to drive the source-backed content-depth activation pattern (`docs/solutions/2026-05-04-source-backed-content-depth-activation-pattern.md`) without needing a stable decision ID — the recipe is the upstream artifact for that pattern. Future agents grepping for `D136` in plan docs or code comments will land here for the explanation; the ID is now a known-removed gap and should not be reassigned.

### Essay 2 — Engaging Your Team / Practice Plan Template (verbatim)

The canonical BAB practice-plan shape. Our 15 / 25 / 40-min session archetypes in `app/src/data/archetypes.ts` are a compressed version of this template.

**Warm-Up (10–15 mins):**

- Set the intention for the day.
- Get the blood flowing with a dynamic warm-up, typically without using a ball.

**Single-Person Drills:**

- Drills designed for one person at a time, usually with a partner. Set reps or time.
- Beginner example: Toss, pass, catch.
- Advanced example: Shuffle passing.

**Two-Person Drills (30–45 mins):**

- Drills where both athletes work on improvement. One position is a "resting" position (though it won't feel like it).
- Beginner example: Two-touch passing. Partner A at net, Partner B in court. A uses one touch to get ball to B, who passes back.
- Advanced example: Shuffle and pass with a downball. A tosses a downball to attack at B; B moves left or right to pass back.

**Team Drills (30–45 mins):**

- Game-like reps while maintaining a specific focus. Fatigue sets in; plan rotations that allow athletes to focus on technical skills.
- Beginner example: Focus pass from coach to sideout hit. Coach tosses for passer to return, followed by serve and attack.
- Advanced example: Add defense after the serve and play it out; optionally keep score.

**Competitive Team Drills (remaining time):**

- Competitive reps with a specific focus. Use a scoring format.
- Example: King/Queen of the court, where the king/queen side must win two balls (one from serve, one from coach's downball).

**Cool Down (10 mins):**

- Analyze progress made during the day.
- Stretch and cool down.

Tier 1 mapping:

- Our `warmup` slot ≈ BAB Warm-Up block (compressed to 3 min via `Beach Prep Three` — `D105`).
- Our `technique` slot ≈ BAB Single-Person Drills block.
- Our `movement_proxy` slot ≈ often a Single-Person or Two-Person drill.
- Our `main_skill` slot ≈ BAB Two-Person or Team Drills (main focus).
- Our `wrap` slot ≈ BAB Cool Down (framed as transition, not recovery — see `D105` and `docs/research/warmup-cooldown-minimum-protocols.md`).

### Essay 3 — Keeping the Competitive Fire (summary)

Three strategies (source captured verbatim; summarized here):

1. **Present a Focus and Prioritize Goal Setting.** Each practice has a focus; each athlete sets a personal goal aligned to that focus.
2. **Maintain Constant Communication.** Use athletes' names frequently. Only stop practice when necessary. Use water breaks for instruction and motivation.
3. **Bring the Energy You Want to See.** If you want a high-intensity, competitive practice, embody that energy.

Tier 1 use: none directly, because M001 is a self-coached product with no coach role. The goal-setting bullet (point 1) is relevant to a **post-M001** weekly-confidence surface (goal on the weekly receipt) and is captured here for that future work. **Tracked as open question `O22` on 2026-05-04** — see `docs/decisions.md` for the M002-scoped resolution criteria (timing of the goal capture, input shape, adaptation coupling, interaction with `D104`, the duplication check vs the existing draft-level reason and carry-forward / next-step lines, and the requirement that any optional goal align to the chosen session focus rather than redefine it; the related single-focus-promotion question itself is tracked as `O24`). Points 2 ("constant communication") and 3 ("bring the energy you want to see") remain non-applicable to a self-coached product and stay captured here as source provenance only — the calm/shibui interface posture and the `P11` recommend-before-interrogate principle pull in a different direction from a coach hype-voice.

| Drill Book Plan 17 Drill 6                                                                                                                                                                                           | Games to 21                                                                                                                                                                                                                             | —                            | Competitive match wrapper format (Tier 3+); session-shape construct, not a drill record. Traditional beach volleyball match scoring with conditional-extension rule (final set to 15 if time remains, regardless of match outcome). Distinct from compressed wrappers (`14-15 Games to 21`), single-set wrappers (`Set to 21`), best-of-N wrappers (`Best of 3, Match to 21`), and modified games (`Mini Games to 7`). Plan 17 introduces conditional-extension as a new composable rule kind — the extension is conditioned on time-remaining, not on match state. Future Volleycraft session-builder logic could distinguish "scheduled" vs "if-time-allows" wrapper extensions                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| Drill Book Plan 18 Drill 4                                                                                                                                                                                           | Triangle Setting with Attack (Serve)                                                                                                                                                                                                    | —                            | **First whole-chain Triangle Setting variant** (Tier 3+). 4-player serve-fed Triangle Setting where P2 passes AND hits the set; P3 and P4 set. | Drill Book Plan 18 Drill 5                                                                                                                                                                                           | Add In/Add Out                                                                                                                                                                                                                          | —                            | **First BAB source detail for wash-drill scoring** (Tier 3+). Pair-vs-pair pressure-game with 4-serve rotation (A1, B1, B2, A2). Points only score when a team wins **consecutive** serve-receive AND serve halves; if conditions split, the result is a wash (no points). **Seventh composable scoring rule kind** — conjunctive/wash scoring with cancellation, distinct from rule-restriction (Plan 8), rule-augmentation (Plans 11/15), tiebreaker (Plan 16), side-switch trigger (Plans 9/17), outcome-elevation gate (Plan 17), and conditional-extension (Plan 17). Plan 6 Drill 7 (`Open Net, High Line, Free. Wash Drill`) was the first BAB use of the term but did not specify scoring mechanics; Plan 18 Drill 5 is the cleanest source. Author the wash-rule as a composable scoring overlay (`scoringRule: conjunctive`) on a base pair-vs-pair sideout drill; future Volleycraft `successMetric` taxonomy needs a new conjunctive/multi-event metric shape distinct from `streak` (consecutive single events) and `reps-successful` (cumulative single events)                                         |
| Drill Book Plan 19 Drill 5                                                                                                                                                                                           | Small Court: Mini Games to 7                                                                                                                                                                                                            | —                            | **First BAB source for scoring-zone gate scoring rule** (Tier 3+). Court-restriction Mini Games to 7 variant: line drawn down center of court dividing each side in half; designated scoring side decided before each game; **every point must be scored on the designated side** (left or right) for the rally outcome to count. **Eighth composable scoring rule kind** — distinct from rule-restriction (which constrains *behavior*), rule-augmentation (Plans 11/15), tiebreaker (Plan 16), side-switch trigger (Plans 9/17), outcome-elevation gate (Plan 17), conditional-extension (Plan 17), and conjunctive/wash (Plan 18). Plan 19 Drill 5 also has a level-scaled rule (beginner/intermediate any-player serve; advanced same-player serve), confirming Thesis T12 across two BAB source cases. Fifth Mini Games to 7 variant in the captured set. Author the court-zone restriction as a composable scoring overlay (`scoringRule: 'zone-gate'` with `zone` parameter) on a base pair-vs-pair sideout drill; future Volleycraft `successMetric` taxonomy needs an outcome-spatial-condition metric shape |
| Drill Book Plan 19 Drill 6                                                                                                                                                                                           | Game to 21 (no regulations)                                                                                                                                                                                                             | —                            | **Cleanest minimal-overlay base form** of the Games to 21 wrapper family (Tier 3+); session-shape construct, not a drill record. Plan 19 explicitly says "no regulations." Confirms BAB has both base forms (this) and overlay variants. Sibling of Plan 17 Drill 6 (`Games to 21` with conditional-extension rule); structurally simpler. Future Volleycraft session-builder logic should treat this as the default Game-to-21 wrapper without overlays, with the **nine** captured composable rule kinds as opt-in modifiers                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| Drill Book Plan 20 Drill 5                                                                                                                                                                                           | 16-18 Run with It                                                                                                                                                                                                                       | —                            | **First BAB source for reset-on-miss / consecutive-streak-required scoring** AND **first BAB source for asymmetric scoring** (Tier 3+). Pair-vs-pair pressure-game where Team A starts at 16, must reach 21 by scoring **consecutively** (any miss resets to 16); Team B accumulates points normally. **Ninth composable scoring rule kind** — reset-on-miss/streak-required, distinct from the eight earlier-captured kinds. **Asymmetric scoring** (different teams, different rules) is also structurally novel — first BAB source for per-team-rule mechanism. Densest single-drill scoring grammar in the captured set: composes four rule kinds (reset-on-miss + asymmetric + win-by-2 + side-switch). Author the asymmetric scoring as `scoringRules: { teamA: 'streak-required-floor-reset', teamB: 'accumulating-normal' }` per-team rather than as a drill-level rule. `successMetric.type` needs a new shape: `streak-required-with-floor-reset`. **Plan 20 completes the captured BAB Drill Book at source-detail level — all 20 plans now captured**                                                     |
| Drill Book Plan 9 (TOC, superseded)                                                                                                                                                                                  | 3 Touch Vision Pepper                                                                                                                                                                                                                   | —                            | Earlier TOC-only entry; superseded by the Plan 9 Drill 3 source-detail row above. Kept for grep-discoverability against the older "Pepper-family content-polish candidate" framing                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |


## How Tier 1 uses these sources

**Tier 1 Unit 1 (warm-up authoring)**: BAB Drill 1 "Best Warm Up Ever" informs the structure of the pair opening-block option (Unit 2), but the Beach Prep Two/Three/Five drills themselves are VDM + physio-reviewed (`D105`, `D129`) and do not clone BAB's 12-minute opener verbatim. Under `D105` our default dose is 3 min of targeted work.

**Tier 1 Unit 2 (pair opening-block)**: `d30 Pair Pepper Progression` clones BAB's cooperative pair-pepper sequence (pass / set / tomahawk / pokey / one-hand pepper / speed pepper) at 10-each cadence. Folds into the warmup slot on pair 25-min and 40-min sessions when the founder toggles it on.

**Tier 1 Unit 3 (serving ladder)**: BAB and VDM supplied the source names and skill-stage gates for the historical serving-ladder plan. The current app catalog only authors the subset that survived later diagnostics and safety/reachability passes; the cross-reference table above marks which IDs are current records versus reserved/planned targets. `d31`'s name comes from the Beginner's Guide Lesson 4 homework drill, and `d33` is the current 6-zone M001 form of BAB's 4 / 6 / 8 Around-the-World serving family. `d35` / `d37` remain source-family planning anchors until an explicit catalog plan authors them.

**Tier 1 Unit 4 (setting chain)**: BAB Beginner's Guide splits setting into Bump Set + Hand Set + Footwork + Principle before any pair drill; Tier 1 Unit 4 mirrors that split. Plan 5 provides the detailed source form for `d40 Footwork for Setting`, and Plan 6 provides the richer source form for `d42 Corner to Corner Setting`. Later 3+ player setting drills remain future provenance rather than current app records. Pair rungs beyond `d40` pull from drill-book practice plans 5 and 6 only where the current app has an authored one/two-player-compatible record.

**No current Tier 1 use of Plans 7-20**: Plans 7–11 are the first five attack-focused practice plans captured at source-detail level, Plans 12–16 are the **complete defense-focused cluster** captured at source-detail level, and **Plans 17, 18, 19, and 20 are the complete Game Play cluster** captured at source-detail level — but none of `attack`, `defense`, or "game play" is a shipped `SkillFocus` and there are no current attack / defense / game-play drills in `app/src/data/drills.ts`. All fourteen plans sit entirely in the Tier 3+ backlog: future attack-chain authoring should consult Plans 7-11 alongside FIVB chapter 5; future defense-chain authoring should consult Plans 12-16 alongside FIVB chapter 7; future game-play / pressure-game wrapper authoring should consult Plans 17-20 alongside FIVB Modified Games chapter 8. **The captured BAB drill book is now structurally complete at source-detail level** — future BAB-related Volleycraft work should treat the captured set as the authoritative reference. The captured BAB defensive technique foundation is now a six-drill set across Plans 12-14, with Plan 15 supplying the live-point integration drill (`Shuffle to HL/CS to Live Play`) and a fourth Mini Games to 7 rule-restriction variant, and Plan 16 supplying the blocker-as-reader read drill pair (`Threat or No Threat` toss-fed and serve-fed siblings). The captured Defensive cluster (Plans 12-16) now provides the **most complete single-focus plan-grammar template** in the BAB set: opener → Triangle Setting (setting touch) → defensive technique foundation → defensive movement (`4 Steps to Paradise`) → smack-misdirection / pull-block / blocker-decision drills → controlled-feed → live-point integration → competitive wrapper. Plan 13 supplies the strongest BAB evidence for drill-repurposing across focus; Plan 14 supplies the first attacker-deception read drill; Plan 16 supplies the first blocker-as-reader read drill (set-quality cue), expanding the read-drill taxonomy to a three-axis schema (reader role × cue source × deceiver role). The accumulated drill-name aliasing cases (Plan 8 `Hitting a HL/CS` ≡ Plan 9 `Offensive Accuracy - HL/CS` ≡ Plan 13 `Toss to HL/CS`; Plan 7 Drill 7 ≡ Plan 10 Drill 8 ≡ Plan 12 Drill 5 ≡ Plan 13 Drill 8 ≡ Plan 14 Drill 6 [five plans]; Plan 9 Drill 7 ≡ Plan 10 Drill 9 ≡ Plan 11 Drill 6 ≡ Plan 13 Drill 9 ≡ Plan 14 Drill 7 ≡ Plan 15 Drill 8 [six plans]; Plan 9 Drill 6 ≡ Plan 11 Drill 5; Plan 2 Drill 4 ≡ Plan 12 Drill 4; Plan 5 Drill 8 ≡ Plan 12 Drill 6; Plan 7 Drill 5 ≡ Plan 13 Drill 7; Plan 12 Drill 2 ≡ Plan 13 Drill 3; Plan 10 Drill 2 ≡ Plan 11 Drill 2 ≡ Plan 14 Drill 2 ≡ Plan 15 Drill 2 [Triangle Setting 4p hit-fed]; Plan 12 Drill 3 ≡ Plan 15 Drill 3 [4 Steps to Paradise]; Plan 14 Drills 4-5 ≡ Plan 15 Drills 4-5 [Shuffle drills]) plus Plan 10's level-scaled rule pattern, Plan 11's rule-augmented variant pattern, Plans 12–13's drill-repurposing-across-focus pattern, Plan 14's smack-misdirection feed pattern, and Plan 15's live-point integration pattern argue for an explicit cross-catalog modeling decision before any attack or defense content lands (see Theses T8 / T9 / T10 / T11 / T12 in `docs/research/practice-plan-authoring-synthesis.md`). The **Mini Games to 7 family** now has at least four documented rule-restriction variants and is the strongest source case yet for the T9 single-base-drill-with-parameter-overlays modeling approach.

**Tier 1 Unit 5 (vocabulary audit)**: Glossary derived directly from the BAB Drill Book practice-plan drill names (see glossary table above).

**Tier 1 Unit 6 (archetype invariants)**: Single-focus invariant cites Essay 1 of the Coaches Guide. Serve-to-attack convertibility invariant cites the drill-book intro.

## Source provenance and citation hygiene

When citing BAB in inline code comments (`app/src/data/drills.ts`, `app/src/data/progressions.ts`), use the shortest specific form that lets a reader find the material:

- **Drill Book**: `// BAB 2024 Drill Book, Practice Plan N Drill M` — e.g. `// BAB 2024 Drill Book, Practice Plan 2 Drill 3` for Serving Spots Around the World.
- **Beginner's Guide**: `// BAB Beginner's Guide, Lesson N — <tutorial or drill name>` — e.g. `// BAB Beginner's Guide, Lesson 4 — Self Toss Target Practice`.
- **Coaches Guide**: `// BAB Coaches Guide — <essay name>` — e.g. `// BAB Coaches Guide — Establishing a Focus`.

Do not paraphrase quotes in code comments — reference the source with a URL or cite this note (`docs/research/bab-source-material.md`). Verbatim quotes live here, not in code.

## What is NOT captured

- Video content from any BAB course (we only have text / TOC captures).
- Full Practice Plan 4 drill-level details — only Drills 5 and 6 are captured in full, Drill 4 is snippet-level, and Drills 1–3 / 7 are repeated-family notes. If Tier 2+ authoring needs exact Drill 4 mechanics, re-solicit the source.
- ~~Practice Plan 20 drill-level details~~ — **closed 2026-05-04 via Plan 20 source capture.** All 20 BAB Drill Book practice plans are now captured at source-detail level. The captured BAB drill book is structurally complete. Plan 20 (the fourth and final Game Play plan) was captured at source-detail level on 2026-05-04, completing the Game Play cluster and the entire 20-plan drill book. Within the captured set, partial captures remain: Plan 4 has only Drills 5 and 6 source-detail captured (Drill 4 snippet, Drills 1-3 / 7 repeated-family notes); Plan 9 Drill 6 source detail was captured via Plan 11 Drill 5; Plans 10-20 each have Drill 1 (Best Warm Up Ever) captured as the standard repeated source family (name-only — Plan 13 Drill 1 carries a parenthetical framing hint `(Dig from Knees)`); Plans 15, 16, 17, 18 have Drill 2 (Triangle Setting) as name-only entries; Plan 20 Drill 2 has truncated source text (first Triangle Setting source-text capture since Plan 14, structurally consistent with the 4-player hit-fed source form from Plans 10/11/14). The slot-4-skip pattern is now confirmed across **all four Game Play plans** (17, 18, 19, 20), and **T10 (read drills) is confirmed absent from the entire Game Play cluster** — narrowing T10 from a universal pattern to a Defense/Attack-only pattern.
- ~~Plan 9 Drill 6 `Beat the Blocker Cross/Line` source detail~~ — **closed 2026-05-04 via Plan 11 Drill 5 source capture.** Plan 11 supplies the full text; Plan 9 Drill 6 and Plan 11 Drill 5 are mapped as aliases of one drill family in the cross-reference table.
- ~~Plan 12 / 15 `4 Steps to Paradise` source detail~~ — **closed 2026-05-04 via Plan 12 Drill 3 source capture.** Plan 12 supplies the full text; the cross-reference row is updated from name-only to source-detail captured. Plan 15's TOC also lists this drill; future Plan 15 source capture would confirm it as repeated source evidence.
- Attacking Lesson 3 homework drills — the source paste captured tutorial names but not homework drills; if Tier 3+ attack chain authoring needs them, re-solicit.
- Defense Lesson content, if one exists separately — not referenced in the 2026-04-20 founder conversation.
